package software.amazon.smithy.model.shapes;

import java.io.Serializable;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.Map;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.FromSourceLocation;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.SourceLocation;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.node.Node;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.traits.TraitDefinition;
import software.amazon.smithy.utils.MapUtils;

/**
 * Defines how shapes, traits, and metadata are sorted when serializing a model with {@link SmithyIdlModelSerializer}.
 */
public enum SmithyIdlComponentOrder {
    /**
     * Sort shapes, traits, and metadata alphabetically. Member order, however, is not sorted.
     */
    ALPHA_NUMERIC,

    /**
     * Sort shapes, traits, and metadata by source location, persisting their original placement when parsed.
     */
    SOURCE_LOCATION,

    /**
     * Reorganizes shapes based on a preferred ordering of shapes, and alphanumeric traits and metadata.
     *
     * <p>Shapes are ordered as follows:
     *
     * <ul>
     *     <li>Trait definitions</li>
     *     <li>Services</li>
     *     <li>Resources</li>
     *     <li>Operations</li>
     *     <li>Structures</li>
     *     <li>Unions</li>
     *     <li>Lists</li>
     *     <li>Maps</li>
     *     <li>Finally, alphabetically by shape type.</li>
     * </ul>
     */
    PREFERRED;

    Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator() {
        return this == PREFERRED ? new PreferredShapeComparator() : toShapeIdComparator();
    }

    <T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId> Comparator<T> toShapeIdComparator() {
        switch (this) {
            case PREFERRED:
            case ALPHA_NUMERIC:
                return Comparator.comparing(ToShapeId::toShapeId);
            case SOURCE_LOCATION:
            default:
                return new SourceComparator<>();
        }
    }

    Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator() {
        switch (this) {
            case ALPHA_NUMERIC:
            case PREFERRED:
                return Map.Entry.comparingByKey();
            case SOURCE_LOCATION:
            default:
                return new MetadataComparator();
        }
    }

    private static final class SourceComparator<T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId>
            implements Comparator<T>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(T a, T b) {
            SourceLocation left = a.getSourceLocation();
            SourceLocation right = b.getSourceLocation();
            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    private static final class MetadataComparator implements Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Map.Entry<String, Node> a, Map.Entry<String, Node> b) {
            SourceLocation left = a.getValue().getSourceLocation();
            SourceLocation right = b.getValue().getSourceLocation();
            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.getKey().compareTo(b.getKey());
        }
    }

    /**
     * Comparator used to sort shapes.
     */
    private static final class PreferredShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
        private static final Map<ShapeType, Integer> PRIORITY = MapUtils.of(
                ShapeType.SERVICE,
                0,
                ShapeType.RESOURCE,
                1,
                ShapeType.OPERATION,
                2,
                ShapeType.STRUCTURE,
                3,
                ShapeType.UNION,
                4,
                ShapeType.LIST,
                5,
                ShapeType.SET,
                6,
                ShapeType.MAP,
                7);

        @Override
        public int compare(Shape s1, Shape s2) {
            // Traits go first
            if (s1.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID) || s2.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                if (!s1.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                    return 1;
                }
                if (!s2.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                    return -1;
                }
                // The other sorting rules don'"'"'t matter for traits.
                return s1.compareTo(s2);
            }
            // If the shapes are the same type, just compare their shape ids.
            if (s1.getType().equals(s2.getType())) {
                return s1.compareTo(s2);
            }
            // If one shape is prioritized, compare by priority.
            if (PRIORITY.containsKey(s1.getType()) || PRIORITY.containsKey(s2.getType())) {
                // If only one shape is prioritized, that shape is "greater".
                if (!PRIORITY.containsKey(s1.getType())) {
                    return 1;
                }
                if (!PRIORITY.containsKey(s2.getType())) {
                    return -1;
                }
                return PRIORITY.get(s1.getType()) - PRIORITY.get(s2.getType());
            }
            return s1.compareTo(s2);
        }
    }
}' --new_str '/*

 * SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

package software.amazon.smithy.model.shapes;

import java.io.Serializable;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.FromSourceLocation;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.SourceLocation;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.node.Node;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.traits.TraitDefinition;
import software.amazon.smithy.utils.MapUtils;

/**
 * Defines how shapes, traits, and metadata are sorted when serializing a model with {@link SmithyIdlModelSerializer}.
 *
 * <p>Users can extend this class by providing custom comparators using the
 * {@link #builder()} method. For example:
 *
 * <pre>{@code
 * SmithyIdlComponentOrder customOrder = SmithyIdlComponentOrder.builder()
 *         .shapeComparator(myShapeComparator)
 *         .traitComparator(myTraitComparator)
 *         .metadataComparator(myMetadataComparator)
 *         .build();
 * }</pre>
 */
public final class SmithyIdlComponentOrder {
    /**
     * Sort shapes, traits, and metadata alphabetically. Member order, however, is not sorted.
     */
    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder ALPHA_NUMERIC = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            new AlphaNumericShapeComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericTraitComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericMetadataComparator()
    );

    /**
     * Sort shapes, traits, and metadata by source location, persisting their original placement when parsed.
     */
    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder SOURCE_LOCATION = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            new SourceShapeComparator(),
            new SourceTraitComparator(),
            new SourceMetadataComparator()
    );

    /**
     * Reorganizes shapes based on a preferred ordering of shapes, and alphanumeric traits and metadata.
     *
     * <p>Shapes are ordered as follows:
     *
     * <ul>
     *     <li>Trait definitions</li>
     *     <li>Services</li>
     *     <li>Resources</li>
     *     <li>Operations</li>
     *     <li>Structures</li>
     *     <li>Unions</li>
     *     <li>Lists</li>
     *     <li>Maps</li>
     *     <li>Finally, alphabetically by shape type.</li>
     * </ul>
     */
    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder PREFERRED = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            new PreferredShapeComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericTraitComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericMetadataComparator()
    );

    private final Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator;
    private final Comparator<Trait> traitComparator;
    private final Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator;

    private SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator,
            Comparator<Trait> traitComparator,
            Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator
    ) {
        this.shapeComparator = shapeComparator;
        this.traitComparator = traitComparator;
        this.metadataComparator = metadataComparator;
    }

    Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator() {
        return shapeComparator;
    }

    <T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId> Comparator<T> toShapeIdComparator() {
        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
        Comparator<T> result = (Comparator<T>) traitComparator;
        return result;
    }

    Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator() {
        return metadataComparator;
    }

    /**
     * Creates a builder used to construct a custom {@link SmithyIdlComponentOrder}.
     *
     * @return Returns a new builder.
     */
    public static Builder builder() {
        return new Builder();
    }

    /**
     * Builder used to create a custom {@link SmithyIdlComponentOrder}.
     */
    public static final class Builder implements SmithyBuilder<SmithyIdlComponentOrder> {
        private Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator;
        private Comparator<Trait> traitComparator;
        private Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator;

        Builder() {}

        /**
         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting shapes.
         *
         * @param shapeComparator Comparator used to sort shapes.
         * @return Returns the builder.
         */
        public Builder shapeComparator(Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator) {
            this.shapeComparator = Objects.requireNonNull(shapeComparator);
            return this;
        }

        /**
         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting traits.
         *
         * @param traitComparator Comparator used to sort traits.
         * @return Returns the builder.
         */
        public Builder traitComparator(Comparator<? extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId> traitComparator) {
            @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
            Comparator<Trait> casted = (Comparator<Trait>) Objects.requireNonNull(traitComparator);
            this.traitComparator = casted;
            return this;
        }

        /**
         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting metadata.
         *
         * @param metadataComparator Comparator used to sort metadata entries.
         * @return Returns the builder.
         */
        public Builder metadataComparator(Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator) {
            this.metadataComparator = Objects.requireNonNull(metadataComparator);
            return this;
        }

        @Override
        public SmithyIdlComponentOrder build() {
            if (shapeComparator == null) {
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("shapeComparator must not be null");
            }
            if (traitComparator == null) {
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("traitComparator must not be null");
            }
            if (metadataComparator == null) {
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("metadataComparator must not be null");
            }
            return new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(shapeComparator, traitComparator, metadataComparator);
        }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Shape comparators
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    private static final class AlphaNumericShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Shape s1, Shape s2) {
            return s1.toShapeId().compareTo(s2.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    private static final class SourceShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Shape a, Shape b) {
            SourceLocation left = a.getSourceLocation();
            SourceLocation right = b.getSourceLocation();
            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    /**
     * Comparator used to sort shapes.
     */
    private static final class PreferredShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
        private static final Map<ShapeType, Integer> PRIORITY = MapUtils.of(
                ShapeType.SERVICE,
                0,
                ShapeType.RESOURCE,
                1,
                ShapeType.OPERATION,
                2,
                ShapeType.STRUCTURE,
                3,
                ShapeType.UNION,
                4,
                ShapeType.LIST,
                5,
                ShapeType.SET,
                6,
                ShapeType.MAP,
                7);

        @Override
        public int compare(Shape s1, Shape s2) {
            // Traits go first
            if (s1.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID) || s2.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                if (!s1.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                    return 1;
                }
                if (!s2.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                    return -1;
                }
                // The other sorting rules don'"'"'t matter for traits.
                return s1.compareTo(s2);
            }
            // If the shapes are the same type, just compare their shape ids.
            if (s1.getType().equals(s2.getType())) {
                return s1.compareTo(s2);
            }
            // If one shape is prioritized, compare by priority.
            if (PRIORITY.containsKey(s1.getType()) || PRIORITY.containsKey(s2.getType())) {
                // If only one shape is prioritized, that shape is "greater".
                if (!PRIORITY.containsKey(s1.getType())) {
                    return 1;
                }
                if (!PRIORITY.containsKey(s2.getType())) {
                    return -1;
                }
                return PRIORITY.get(s1.getType()) - PRIORITY.get(s2.getType());
            }
            return s1.compareTo(s2);
        }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Trait comparators
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    private static final class AlphaNumericTraitComparator<T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId>
            implements Comparator<T>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(T a, T b) {
            return a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    private static final class SourceTraitComparator<T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId>
            implements Comparator<T>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(T a, T b) {
            SourceLocation left = a.getSourceLocation();
            SourceLocation right = b.getSourceLocation();
            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Metadata comparators
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    private static final class AlphaNumericMetadataComparator
            implements Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Map.Entry<String, Node> a, Map.Entry<String, Node> b) {
            return a.getKey().compareTo(b.getKey());
        }
    }

    private static final class SourceMetadataComparator
            implements Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Map.Entry<String, Node> a, Map.Entry<String, Node> b) {
            SourceLocation left = a.getValue().getSourceLocation();
            SourceLocation right = b.getValue().getSourceLocation();
            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.getKey().compareTo(b.getKey());
        }
    }
}'

/*
 * Copyright Amazon.com, Inc. or its affiliates. All Rights Reserved.
 * SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
 */
package software.amazon.smithy.model.shapes;

import java.io.Serializable;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.FromSourceLocation;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.SourceLocation;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.node.Node;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.traits.TraitDefinition;
import software.amazon.smithy.utils.MapUtils;

/**
 * Defines how shapes, traits, and metadata are sorted when serializing a model with {@link SmithyIdlModelSerializer}.
 *
 * <p>Users can extend this class by providing custom comparators using the
 * {@link #builder()} method. For example:
 *
 * <pre>{@code
 * SmithyIdlComponentOrder customOrder = SmithyIdlComponentOrder.builder()
 *         .shapeComparator(myShapeComparator)
 *         .traitComparator(myTraitComparator)
 *         .metadataComparator(myMetadataComparator)
 *         .build();
 * }</pre>
 */
public final class SmithyIdlComponentOrder {
    /**
     * Sort shapes, traits, and metadata alphabetically. Member order, however, is not sorted.
     */
    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder ALPHA_NUMERIC = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            new AlphaNumericShapeComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericTraitComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericMetadataComparator()
    );

    /**
     * Sort shapes, traits, and metadata by source location, persisting their original placement when parsed.
     */
    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder SOURCE_LOCATION = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            new SourceShapeComparator(),
            new SourceTraitComparator(),
            new SourceMetadataComparator()
    );

    /**
     * Reorganizes shapes based on a preferred ordering of shapes, and alphanumeric traits and metadata.
     *
     * <p>Shapes are ordered as follows:
     *
     * <ul>
     *     <li>Trait definitions</li>
     *     <li>Services</li>
     *     <li>Resources</li>
     *     <li>Operations</li>
     *     <li>Structures</li>
     *     <li>Unions</li>
     *     <li>Lists</li>
     *     <li>Maps</li>
     *     <li>Finally, alphabetically by shape type.</li>
     * </ul>
     */
    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder PREFERRED = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            new PreferredShapeComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericTraitComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericMetadataComparator()
    );

    private final Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator;
    private final Comparator<Trait> traitComparator;
    private final Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator;

    private SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator,
            Comparator<Trait> traitComparator,
            Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator
    ) {
        this.shapeComparator = shapeComparator;
        this.traitComparator = traitComparator;
        this.metadataComparator = metadataComparator;
    }

    Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator() {
        return shapeComparator;
    }

    <T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId> Comparator<T> toShapeIdComparator() {
        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
        Comparator<T> result = (Comparator<T>) traitComparator;
        return result;
    }

    Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator() {
        return metadataComparator;
    }

    /**
     * Creates a builder used to construct a custom {@link SmithyIdlComponentOrder}.
     *
     * @return Returns a new builder.
     */
    public static Builder builder() {
        return new Builder();
    }

    /**
     * Builder used to create a custom {@link SmithyIdlComponentOrder}.
     */
    public static final class Builder implements SmithyBuilder<SmithyIdlComponentOrder> {
        private Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator;
        private Comparator<Trait> traitComparator;
        private Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator;

        Builder() {}

        /**
         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting shapes.
         *
         * @param shapeComparator Comparator used to sort shapes.
         * @return Returns the builder.
         */
        public Builder shapeComparator(Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator) {
            this.shapeComparator = Objects.requireNonNull(shapeComparator);
            return this;
        }

        /**
         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting traits.
         *
         * @param traitComparator Comparator used to sort traits.
         * @return Returns the builder.
         */
        public Builder traitComparator(Comparator<? extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId> traitComparator) {
            @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
            Comparator<Trait> casted = (Comparator<Trait>) Objects.requireNonNull(traitComparator);
            this.traitComparator = casted;
            return this;
        }

        /**
         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting metadata.
         *
         * @param metadataComparator Comparator used to sort metadata entries.
         * @return Returns the builder.
         */
        public Builder metadataComparator(Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator) {
            this.metadataComparator = Objects.requireNonNull(metadataComparator);
            return this;
        }

        @Override
        public SmithyIdlComponentOrder build() {
            if (shapeComparator == null) {
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("shapeComparator must not be null");
            }
            if (traitComparator == null) {
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("traitComparator must not be null");
            }
            if (metadataComparator == null) {
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("metadataComparator must not be null");
            }
            return new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(shapeComparator, traitComparator, metadataComparator);
        }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Shape comparators
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    private static final class AlphaNumericShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Shape s1, Shape s2) {
            return s1.toShapeId().compareTo(s2.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    private static final class SourceShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Shape a, Shape b) {
            SourceLocation left = a.getSourceLocation();
            SourceLocation right = b.getSourceLocation();
            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    /**
     * Comparator used to sort shapes.
     */
    private static final class PreferredShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
        private static final Map<ShapeType, Integer> PRIORITY = MapUtils.of(
                ShapeType.SERVICE,
                0,
                ShapeType.RESOURCE,
                1,
                ShapeType.OPERATION,
                2,
                ShapeType.STRUCTURE,
                3,
                ShapeType.UNION,
                4,
                ShapeType.LIST,
                5,
                ShapeType.SET,
                6,
                ShapeType.MAP,
                7);

        @Override
        public int compare(Shape s1, Shape s2) {
            // Traits go first
            if (s1.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID) || s2.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                if (!s1.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                    return 1;
                }
                if (!s2.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                    return -1;
                }
                // The other sorting rules don't matter for traits.
                return s1.compareTo(s2);
            }
            // If the shapes are the same type, just compare their shape ids.
            if (s1.getType().equals(s2.getType())) {
                return s1.compareTo(s2);
            }
            // If one shape is prioritized, compare by priority.
            if (PRIORITY.containsKey(s1.getType()) || PRIORITY.containsKey(s2.getType())) {
                // If only one shape is prioritized, that shape is "greater".
                if (!PRIORITY.containsKey(s1.getType())) {
                    return 1;
                }
                if (!PRIORITY.containsKey(s2.getType())) {
                    return -1;
                }
                return PRIORITY.get(s1.getType()) - PRIORITY.get(s2.getType());
            }
            return s1.compareTo(s2);
        }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Trait comparators
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    private static final class AlphaNumericTraitComparator<T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId>
            implements Comparator<T>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(T a, T b) {
            return a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    private static final class SourceTraitComparator<T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId>
            implements Comparator<T>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(T a, T b) {
            SourceLocation left = a.getSourceLocation();
            SourceLocation right = b.getSourceLocation();
            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Metadata comparators
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    private static final class AlphaNumericMetadataComparator
            implements Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Map.Entry<String, Node> a, Map.Entry<String, Node> b) {
            return a.getKey().compareTo(b.getKey());
        }
    }

    private static final class SourceMetadataComparator
            implements Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Map.Entry<String, Node> a, Map.Entry<String, Node> b) {
            SourceLocation left = a.getValue().getSourceLocation();
            SourceLocation right = b.getValue().getSourceLocation();
            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.getKey().compareTo(b.getKey());
        }
    }
}

2026-05-30 02:38:47,778 - INFO - swea-agent-smithy-lang__smithy-3058 - 💭 THOUGHT
The issue is that Java can't use `&` in a type parameter bound with a wildcard. Let me fix the generics in the builder method. Since `Trait` implements both `FromSourceLocation` and `ToShapeId`, the `toShapeIdComparator()` is used for traits. The method signature in the builder should accept `Comparator<Trait>` directly, or we can use a different approach.

Let me think about this... The `toShapeIdComparator()` method returns `Comparator<T>` where `T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId`. In the old code, it was called with `Trait` values. So the trait comparator should be `Comparator<Trait>` internally.

But for the builder, to make it easier for users, we can accept `Comparator<Trait>` directly. However, the more flexible approach is to accept `Comparator<? extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId>` but Java doesn't allow intersection types with wildcards.

Let me simplify: accept `Comparator<Trait>` directly since that's the concrete type used:



🎬 ACTION
cat > /testbed/smithy-model/src/main/java/software/amazon/smithy/model/shapes/SmithyIdlComponentOrder.java << 'EOF'
/*
 * Copyright Amazon.com, Inc. or its affiliates. All Rights Reserved.
 * SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
 */
package software.amazon.smithy.model.shapes;

import java.io.Serializable;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.FromSourceLocation;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.SourceLocation;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.node.Node;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.traits.Trait;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.traits.TraitDefinition;
import software.amazon.smithy.utils.MapUtils;

/**
 * Defines how shapes, traits, and metadata are sorted when serializing a model with {@link SmithyIdlModelSerializer}.
 *
 * <p>Users can extend this class by providing custom comparators using the
 * {@link #builder()} method. For example:
 *
 * <pre>{@code
 * SmithyIdlComponentOrder customOrder = SmithyIdlComponentOrder.builder()
 *         .shapeComparator(myShapeComparator)
 *         .traitComparator(myTraitComparator)
 *         .metadataComparator(myMetadataComparator)
 *         .build();
 * }</pre>
 */
public final class SmithyIdlComponentOrder {
    /**
     * Sort shapes, traits, and metadata alphabetically. Member order, however, is not sorted.
     */
    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder ALPHA_NUMERIC = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            new AlphaNumericShapeComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericTraitComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericMetadataComparator()
    );

    /**
     * Sort shapes, traits, and metadata by source location, persisting their original placement when parsed.
     */
    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder SOURCE_LOCATION = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            new SourceShapeComparator(),
            new SourceTraitComparator(),
            new SourceMetadataComparator()
    );

    /**
     * Reorganizes shapes based on a preferred ordering of shapes, and alphanumeric traits and metadata.
     *
     * <p>Shapes are ordered as follows:
     *
     * <ul>
     *     <li>Trait definitions</li>
     *     <li>Services</li>
     *     <li>Resources</li>
     *     <li>Operations</li>
     *     <li>Structures</li>
     *     <li>Unions</li>
     *     <li>Lists</li>
     *     <li>Maps</li>
     *     <li>Finally, alphabetically by shape type.</li>
     * </ul>
     */
    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder PREFERRED = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            new PreferredShapeComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericTraitComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericMetadataComparator()
    );

    private final Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator;
    private final Comparator<Trait> traitComparator;
    private final Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator;

    private SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator,
            Comparator<Trait> traitComparator,
            Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator
    ) {
        this.shapeComparator = shapeComparator;
        this.traitComparator = traitComparator;
        this.metadataComparator = metadataComparator;
    }

    Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator() {
        return shapeComparator;
    }

    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    <T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId> Comparator<T> toShapeIdComparator() {
        return (Comparator<T>) traitComparator;
    }

    Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator() {
        return metadataComparator;
    }

    /**
     * Creates a builder used to construct a custom {@link SmithyIdlComponentOrder}.
     *
     * @return Returns a new builder.
     */
    public static Builder builder() {
        return new Builder();
    }

    /**
     * Builder used to create a custom {@link SmithyIdlComponentOrder}.
     */
    public static final class Builder implements SmithyBuilder<SmithyIdlComponentOrder> {
        private Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator;
        private Comparator<Trait> traitComparator;
        private Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator;

        Builder() {}

        /**
         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting shapes.
         *
         * @param shapeComparator Comparator used to sort shapes.
         * @return Returns the builder.
         */
        public Builder shapeComparator(Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator) {
            this.shapeComparator = Objects.requireNonNull(shapeComparator);
            return this;
        }

        /**
         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting traits.
         *
         * @param traitComparator Comparator used to sort traits.
         * @return Returns the builder.
         */
        public Builder traitComparator(Comparator<Trait> traitComparator) {
            this.traitComparator = Objects.requireNonNull(traitComparator);
            return this;
        }

        /**
         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting metadata.
         *
         * @param metadataComparator Comparator used to sort metadata entries.
         * @return Returns the builder.
         */
        public Builder metadataComparator(Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator) {
            this.metadataComparator = Objects.requireNonNull(metadataComparator);
            return this;
        }

        @Override
        public SmithyIdlComponentOrder build() {
            if (shapeComparator == null) {
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("shapeComparator must not be null");
            }
            if (traitComparator == null) {
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("traitComparator must not be null");
            }
            if (metadataComparator == null) {
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("metadataComparator must not be null");
            }
            return new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(shapeComparator, traitComparator, metadataComparator);
        }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Shape comparators
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    private static final class AlphaNumericShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Shape s1, Shape s2) {
            return s1.toShapeId().compareTo(s2.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    private static final class SourceShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Shape a, Shape b) {
            SourceLocation left = a.getSourceLocation();
            SourceLocation right = b.getSourceLocation();
            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    /**
     * Comparator used to sort shapes.
     */
    private static final class PreferredShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
        private static final Map<ShapeType, Integer> PRIORITY = MapUtils.of(
                ShapeType.SERVICE,
                0,
                ShapeType.RESOURCE,
                1,
                ShapeType.OPERATION,
                2,
                ShapeType.STRUCTURE,
                3,
                ShapeType.UNION,
                4,
                ShapeType.LIST,
                5,
                ShapeType.SET,
                6,
                ShapeType.MAP,
                7);

        @Override
        public int compare(Shape s1, Shape s2) {
            // Traits go first
            if (s1.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID) || s2.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                if (!s1.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                    return 1;
                }
                if (!s2.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                    return -1;
                }
                // The other sorting rules don't matter for traits.
                return s1.compareTo(s2);
            }
            // If the shapes are the same type, just compare their shape ids.
            if (s1.getType().equals(s2.getType())) {
                return s1.compareTo(s2);
            }
            // If one shape is prioritized, compare by priority.
            if (PRIORITY.containsKey(s1.getType()) || PRIORITY.containsKey(s2.getType())) {
                // If only one shape is prioritized, that shape is "greater".
                if (!PRIORITY.containsKey(s1.getType())) {
                    return 1;
                }
                if (!PRIORITY.containsKey(s2.getType())) {
                    return -1;
                }
                return PRIORITY.get(s1.getType()) - PRIORITY.get(s2.getType());
            }
            return s1.compareTo(s2);
        }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Trait comparators
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    private static final class AlphaNumericTraitComparator<T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId>
            implements Comparator<T>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(T a, T b) {
            return a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    private static final class SourceTraitComparator<T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId>
            implements Comparator<T>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(T a, T b) {
            SourceLocation left = a.getSourceLocation();
            SourceLocation right = b.getSourceLocation();
            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Metadata comparators
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    private static final class AlphaNumericMetadataComparator
            implements Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Map.Entry<String, Node> a, Map.Entry<String, Node> b) {
            return a.getKey().compareTo(b.getKey());
        }
    }

    private static final class SourceMetadataComparator
            implements Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Map.Entry<String, Node> a, Map.Entry<String, Node> b) {
            SourceLocation left = a.getValue().getSourceLocation();
            SourceLocation right = b.getValue().getSourceLocation();
            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.getKey().compareTo(b.getKey());
        }
    }
}

     5	package software.amazon.smithy.model.shapes;
     6	
     7	import java.io.Serializable;
     8	import java.util.Comparator;
     9	import java.util.Map;
    10	import java.util.Objects;
    11	import software.amazon.smithy.model.FromSourceLocation;
    12	import software.amazon.smithy.model.SourceLocation;
    13	import software.amazon.smithy.model.node.Node;
    14	import software.amazon.smithy.model.traits.Trait;
    15	import software.amazon.smithy.model.traits.TraitDefinition;
    16	import software.amazon.smithy.utils.MapUtils;
    17	import software.amazon.smithy.utils.SmithyBuilder;
    18	
    19	/**
    20	 * Defines how shapes, traits, and metadata are sorted when serializing a model with {@link SmithyIdlModelSerializer}.
    21	 *
    22	 * <p>Users can extend this class by providing custom comparators using the
    23	 * {@link #builder()} method. For example:
    24	 *
    25	 * <pre>{@code
    26	 * SmithyIdlComponentOrder customOrder = SmithyIdlComponentOrder.builder()
    27	 *         .shapeComparator(myShapeComparator)
    28	 *         .traitComparator(myTraitComparator)
    29	 *         .metadataComparator(myMetadataComparator)
    30	 *         .build();
    31	 * }</pre>
    32	 */
    33	public final class SmithyIdlComponentOrder {
    34	    /**
    35	     * Sort shapes, traits, and metadata alphabetically. Member order, however, is not sorted.
    36	     */
    37	    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder ALPHA_NUMERIC = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
    38	            new AlphaNumericShapeComparator(),
    39	            new AlphaNumericTraitComparator(),
    40	            new AlphaNumericMetadataComparator()
    41	    );
    42	
    43	    /**
    44	     * Sort shapes, traits, and metadata by source location, persisting their original placement when parsed.
    45	     */
    46	    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder SOURCE_LOCATION = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
    47	            new SourceShapeComparator(),
    48	            new SourceTraitComparator(),
    49	            new SourceMetadataComparator()
    50	    );
    51	
    52	    /**
    53	     * Reorganizes shapes based on a preferred ordering of shapes, and alphanumeric traits and metadata.
    54	     *
    55	     * <p>Shapes are ordered as follows:
    56	     *
    57	     * <ul>
    58	     *     <li>Trait definitions</li>
    59	     *     <li>Services</li>
    60	     *     <li>Resources</li>
    61	     *     <li>Operations</li>
    62	     *     <li>Structures</li>
    63	     *     <li>Unions</li>
    64	     *     <li>Lists</li>
    65	     *     <li>Maps</li>
    66	     *     <li>Finally, alphabetically by shape type.</li>
    67	     * </ul>
    68	     */
    69	    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder PREFERRED = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
    70	            new PreferredShapeComparator(),
    71	            new AlphaNumericTraitComparator(),
    72	            new AlphaNumericMetadataComparator()
    73	    );
    74	
    75	    private final Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator;
    76	    private final Comparator<Trait> traitComparator;
    77	    private final Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator;
    78	
    79	    private SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
    80	            Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator,
    81	            Comparator<Trait> traitComparator,
    82	            Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator
    83	    ) {
    84	        this.shapeComparator = shapeComparator;
    85	        this.traitComparator = traitComparator;
    86	        this.metadataComparator = metadataComparator;
    87	    }
    88	
    89	    Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator() {
    90	        return shapeComparator;
    91	    }
    92	
    93	    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    94	    <T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId> Comparator<T> toShapeIdComparator() {
    95	        return (Comparator<T>) traitComparator;
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator() {
    99	        return metadataComparator;
   100	    }
   101	
   102	    /**
   103	     * Creates a builder used to construct a custom {@link SmithyIdlComponentOrder}.
   104	     *
   105	     * @return Returns a new builder.
   106	     */
   107	    public static Builder builder() {
   108	        return new Builder();
   109	    }
   110	
   111	    /**
   112	     * Builder used to create a custom {@link SmithyIdlComponentOrder}.
   113	     */
   114	    public static final class Builder implements SmithyBuilder<SmithyIdlComponentOrder> {
   115	        private Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator;
   116	        private Comparator<Trait> traitComparator;
   117	        private Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator;
   118	
   119	        Builder() {}
   120	
   121	        /**
   122	         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting shapes.
   123	         *
   124	         * @param shapeComparator Comparator used to sort shapes.
   125	         * @return Returns the builder.
   126	         */
   127	        public Builder shapeComparator(Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator) {
   128	            this.shapeComparator = Objects.requireNonNull(shapeComparator);
   129	            return this;
   130	        }
   131	
   132	        /**
   133	         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting traits.
   134	         *
   135	         * @param traitComparator Comparator used to sort traits.
   136	         * @return Returns the builder.
   137	         */
   138	        public Builder traitComparator(Comparator<Trait> traitComparator) {
   139	            this.traitComparator = Objects.requireNonNull(traitComparator);
   140	            return this;
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        /**
   144	         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting metadata.
   145	         *
   146	         * @param metadataComparator Comparator used to sort metadata entries.
   147	         * @return Returns the builder.
   148	         */
   149	        public Builder metadataComparator(Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator) {
   150	            this.metadataComparator = Objects.requireNonNull(metadataComparator);
   151	            return this;
   152	        }
   153	
   154	        @Override
   155	        public SmithyIdlComponentOrder build() {
   156	            if (shapeComparator == null) {
   157	                throw new IllegalArgumentException("shapeComparator must not be null");
   158	            }
   159	            if (traitComparator == null) {
   160	                throw new IllegalArgumentException("traitComparator must not be null");
   161	            }
   162	            if (metadataComparator == null) {
   163	                throw new IllegalArgumentException("metadataComparator must not be null");
   164	            }
   165	            return new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(shapeComparator, traitComparator, metadataComparator);
   166	        }
   167	    }
   168	
   169	    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   170	    // Shape comparators
   171	    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   172	
   173	    private static final class AlphaNumericShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
   174	        @Override
   175	        public int compare(Shape s1, Shape s2) {
   176	            return s1.toShapeId().compareTo(s2.toShapeId());
   177	        }
   178	    }
   179	
   180	    private static final class SourceShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
   181	        @Override
   182	        public int compare(Shape a, Shape b) {
   183	            SourceLocation left = a.getSourceLocation();
   184	            SourceLocation right = b.getSourceLocation();
   185	            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
   186	            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
   187	        }
   188	    }
   189	
   190	    /**
   191	     * Comparator used to sort shapes.
   192	     */
   193	    private static final class PreferredShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
   194	        private static final Map<ShapeType, Integer> PRIORITY = MapUtils.of(
   195	                ShapeType.SERVICE,
   196	                0,
   197	                ShapeType.RESOURCE,
   198	                1,
   199	                ShapeType.OPERATION,
   200	                2,
   201	                ShapeType.STRUCTURE,
   202	                3,
   203	                ShapeType.UNION,
   204	                4,
   205	                ShapeType.LIST,
   206	                5,
   207	                ShapeType.SET,
   208	                6,
   209	                ShapeType.MAP,
   210	                7);
   211	
   212	        @Override
   213	        public int compare(Shape s1, Shape s2) {
   214	            // Traits go first
   215	            if (s1.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID) || s2.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
   216	                if (!s1.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
   217	                    return 1;
   218	                }
   219	                if (!s2.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
   220	                    return -1;
   221	                }
   222	                // The other sorting rules don't matter for traits.
   223	                return s1.compareTo(s2);
   224	            }
   225	            // If the shapes are the same type, just compare their shape ids.
   226	            if (s1.getType().equals(s2.getType())) {
   227	                return s1.compareTo(s2);
   228	            }
   229	            // If one shape is prioritized, compare by priority.
   230	            if (PRIORITY.containsKey(s1.getType()) || PRIORITY.containsKey(s2.getType())) {
   231	                // If only one shape is prioritized, that shape is "greater".
   232	                if (!PRIORITY.containsKey(s1.getType())) {
   233	                    return 1;
   234	                }
   235	                if (!PRIORITY.containsKey(s2.getType())) {
   236	                    return -1;
   237	                }
   238	                return PRIORITY.get(s1.getType()) - PRIORITY.get(s2.getType());
   239	            }
   240	            return s1.compareTo(s2);
   241	        }
   242	    }
   243	
   244	    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   245	    // Trait comparators
   246	    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   247	
   248	    private static final class AlphaNumericTraitComparator<T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId>
   249	            implements Comparator<T>, Serializable {
   250	        @Override
   251	        public int compare(T a, T b) {
   252	            return a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
   253	        }
   254	    }
   255	
   256	    private static final class SourceTraitComparator<T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId>
   257	            implements Comparator<T>, Serializable {
   258	        @Override
   259	        public int compare(T a, T b) {
   260	            SourceLocation left = a.getSourceLocation();
   261	            SourceLocation right = b.getSourceLocation();
   262	            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
   263	            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
   264	        }
   265	    }
   266	
   267	    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   268	    // Metadata comparators
   269	    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   270	
   271	    private static final class AlphaNumericMetadataComparator
   272	            implements Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>>, Serializable {
   273	        @Override
   274	        public int compare(Map.Entry<String, Node> a, Map.Entry<String, Node> b) {
   275	            return a.getKey().compareTo(b.getKey());
   276	        }
   277	    }
   278	
   279	    private static final class SourceMetadataComparator
   280	            implements Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>>, Serializable {
   281	        @Override
   282	        public int compare(Map.Entry<String, Node> a, Map.Entry<String, Node> b) {
   283	            SourceLocation left = a.getValue().getSourceLocation();
   284	            SourceLocation right = b.getValue().getSourceLocation();
   285	            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
   286	            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.getKey().compareTo(b.getKey());
   287	        }
   288	    }
   289	}

import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.Map;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.shapes.SmithyIdlComponentOrder;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.shapes.Shape;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.traits.Trait;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.node.Node;

public class TestCustomOrder {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        // Test 1: Use built-in constants
        System.out.println("ALPHA_NUMERIC: " + SmithyIdlComponentOrder.ALPHA_NUMERIC);
        System.out.println("SOURCE_LOCATION: " + SmithyIdlComponentOrder.SOURCE_LOCATION);
        System.out.println("PREFERRED: " + SmithyIdlComponentOrder.PREFERRED);
        
        // Test 2: Build a custom order
        Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator = (s1, s2) -> s1.toShapeId().compareTo(s2.toShapeId());
        Comparator<Trait> traitComparator = (t1, t2) -> t1.toShapeId().compareTo(t2.toShapeId());
        Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator = Map.Entry.comparingByKey();
        
        SmithyIdlComponentOrder customOrder = SmithyIdlComponentOrder.builder()
                .shapeComparator(shapeComparator)
                .traitComparator(traitComparator)
                .metadataComparator(metadataComparator)
                .build();
        
        System.out.println("Custom order built successfully: " + customOrder);
        System.out.println("Shape comparator: " + customOrder.shapeComparator());
        System.out.println("Trait comparator: " + customOrder.toShapeIdComparator());
        System.out.println("Metadata comparator: " + customOrder.metadataComparator());
        
        System.out.println("All tests passed!");
    }
}

/*
 * Copyright Amazon.com, Inc. or its affiliates. All Rights Reserved.
 * SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
 */
package software.amazon.smithy.model.shapes;

import java.io.Serializable;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.FromSourceLocation;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.SourceLocation;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.node.Node;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.traits.Trait;
import software.amazon.smithy.model.traits.TraitDefinition;
import software.amazon.smithy.utils.MapUtils;
import software.amazon.smithy.utils.SmithyBuilder;

/**
 * Defines how shapes, traits, and metadata are sorted when serializing a model with {@link SmithyIdlModelSerializer}.
 *
 * <p>Users can extend this class by providing custom comparators using the
 * {@link #builder()} method. For example:
 *
 * <pre>{@code
 * SmithyIdlComponentOrder customOrder = SmithyIdlComponentOrder.builder()
 *         .shapeComparator(myShapeComparator)
 *         .traitComparator(myTraitComparator)
 *         .metadataComparator(myMetadataComparator)
 *         .build();
 * }</pre>
 */
public final class SmithyIdlComponentOrder {
    /**
     * Sort shapes, traits, and metadata alphabetically. Member order, however, is not sorted.
     */
    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder ALPHA_NUMERIC = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            new AlphaNumericShapeComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericTraitComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericMetadataComparator()
    );

    /**
     * Sort shapes, traits, and metadata by source location, persisting their original placement when parsed.
     */
    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder SOURCE_LOCATION = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            new SourceShapeComparator(),
            new SourceTraitComparator(),
            new SourceMetadataComparator()
    );

    /**
     * Reorganizes shapes based on a preferred ordering of shapes, and alphanumeric traits and metadata.
     *
     * <p>Shapes are ordered as follows:
     *
     * <ul>
     *     <li>Trait definitions</li>
     *     <li>Services</li>
     *     <li>Resources</li>
     *     <li>Operations</li>
     *     <li>Structures</li>
     *     <li>Unions</li>
     *     <li>Lists</li>
     *     <li>Maps</li>
     *     <li>Finally, alphabetically by shape type.</li>
     * </ul>
     */
    public static final SmithyIdlComponentOrder PREFERRED = new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            new PreferredShapeComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericTraitComparator(),
            new AlphaNumericMetadataComparator()
    );

    private final Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator;
    private final Comparator<Trait> traitComparator;
    private final Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator;

    private SmithyIdlComponentOrder(
            Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator,
            Comparator<Trait> traitComparator,
            Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator
    ) {
        this.shapeComparator = shapeComparator;
        this.traitComparator = traitComparator;
        this.metadataComparator = metadataComparator;
    }

    Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator() {
        return shapeComparator;
    }

    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    <T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId> Comparator<T> toShapeIdComparator() {
        return (Comparator<T>) traitComparator;
    }

    Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator() {
        return metadataComparator;
    }

    /**
     * Creates a builder used to construct a custom {@link SmithyIdlComponentOrder}.
     *
     * @return Returns a new builder.
     */
    public static Builder builder() {
        return new Builder();
    }

    /**
     * Builder used to create a custom {@link SmithyIdlComponentOrder}.
     */
    public static final class Builder implements SmithyBuilder<SmithyIdlComponentOrder> {
        private Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator;
        private Comparator<Trait> traitComparator;
        private Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator;

        Builder() {}

        /**
         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting shapes.
         *
         * @param shapeComparator Comparator used to sort shapes.
         * @return Returns the builder.
         */
        public Builder shapeComparator(Comparator<Shape> shapeComparator) {
            this.shapeComparator = Objects.requireNonNull(shapeComparator);
            return this;
        }

        /**
         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting traits.
         *
         * @param traitComparator Comparator used to sort traits.
         * @return Returns the builder.
         */
        public Builder traitComparator(Comparator<Trait> traitComparator) {
            this.traitComparator = Objects.requireNonNull(traitComparator);
            return this;
        }

        /**
         * Sets a custom comparator for sorting metadata.
         *
         * @param metadataComparator Comparator used to sort metadata entries.
         * @return Returns the builder.
         */
        public Builder metadataComparator(Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>> metadataComparator) {
            this.metadataComparator = Objects.requireNonNull(metadataComparator);
            return this;
        }

        @Override
        public SmithyIdlComponentOrder build() {
            if (shapeComparator == null) {
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("shapeComparator must not be null");
            }
            if (traitComparator == null) {
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("traitComparator must not be null");
            }
            if (metadataComparator == null) {
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("metadataComparator must not be null");
            }
            return new SmithyIdlComponentOrder(shapeComparator, traitComparator, metadataComparator);
        }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Shape comparators
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    private static final class AlphaNumericShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Shape s1, Shape s2) {
            return s1.toShapeId().compareTo(s2.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    private static final class SourceShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Shape a, Shape b) {
            SourceLocation left = a.getSourceLocation();
            SourceLocation right = b.getSourceLocation();
            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    /**
     * Comparator used to sort shapes.
     */
    private static final class PreferredShapeComparator implements Comparator<Shape>, Serializable {
        private static final Map<ShapeType, Integer> PRIORITY = MapUtils.of(
                ShapeType.SERVICE,
                0,
                ShapeType.RESOURCE,
                1,
                ShapeType.OPERATION,
                2,
                ShapeType.STRUCTURE,
                3,
                ShapeType.UNION,
                4,
                ShapeType.LIST,
                5,
                ShapeType.SET,
                6,
                ShapeType.MAP,
                7);

        @Override
        public int compare(Shape s1, Shape s2) {
            // Traits go first
            if (s1.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID) || s2.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                if (!s1.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                    return 1;
                }
                if (!s2.hasTrait(TraitDefinition.ID)) {
                    return -1;
                }
                // The other sorting rules don't matter for traits.
                return s1.compareTo(s2);
            }
            // If the shapes are the same type, just compare their shape ids.
            if (s1.getType().equals(s2.getType())) {
                return s1.compareTo(s2);
            }
            // If one shape is prioritized, compare by priority.
            if (PRIORITY.containsKey(s1.getType()) || PRIORITY.containsKey(s2.getType())) {
                // If only one shape is prioritized, that shape is "greater".
                if (!PRIORITY.containsKey(s1.getType())) {
                    return 1;
                }
                if (!PRIORITY.containsKey(s2.getType())) {
                    return -1;
                }
                return PRIORITY.get(s1.getType()) - PRIORITY.get(s2.getType());
            }
            return s1.compareTo(s2);
        }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Trait comparators
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    private static final class AlphaNumericTraitComparator<T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId>
            implements Comparator<T>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(T a, T b) {
            return a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    private static final class SourceTraitComparator<T extends FromSourceLocation & ToShapeId>
            implements Comparator<T>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(T a, T b) {
            SourceLocation left = a.getSourceLocation();
            SourceLocation right = b.getSourceLocation();
            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.toShapeId().compareTo(b.toShapeId());
        }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Metadata comparators
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    private static final class AlphaNumericMetadataComparator
            implements Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Map.Entry<String, Node> a, Map.Entry<String, Node> b) {
            return a.getKey().compareTo(b.getKey());
        }
    }

    private static final class SourceMetadataComparator
            implements Comparator<Map.Entry<String, Node>>, Serializable {
        @Override
        public int compare(Map.Entry<String, Node> a, Map.Entry<String, Node> b) {
            SourceLocation left = a.getValue().getSourceLocation();
            SourceLocation right = b.getValue().getSourceLocation();
            int comparison = left.compareTo(right);
            return comparison != 0 ? comparison : a.getKey().compareTo(b.getKey());
        }
    }
}

#!/usr/bin/env python3

import argparse
from pathlib import Path
import subprocess
import sys
import os
import io

from registry import registry


def main() -> None:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Submit changes for review")
    parser.add_argument("-f", "--force", action="store_true", help="Force submit without review")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    repo_root = registry.get("ROOT", os.getenv("ROOT"))
    assert repo_root

    patch_path = Path("/root/model.patch")

    subprocess.run(
        f"git add -A && git diff --cached > {patch_path}",
        shell=True,
        stdout=subprocess.DEVNULL,
        stderr=subprocess.DEVNULL,
        cwd=repo_root,
    )

    patch = patch_path.read_text(errors="backslashreplace")

    submit_review_messages = registry.get("SUBMIT_REVIEW_MESSAGES", [])
    n_stages = len(submit_review_messages)
    current_stage = registry.get("SUBMIT_STAGE", 0)
    if not args.force and current_stage != n_stages:
        message = submit_review_messages[current_stage]
        message = message.replace("{{diff}}", patch)
        message = message.replace("{{problem_statement}}", registry.get("PROBLEM_STATEMENT", ""))
        registry["SUBMIT_STAGE"] = current_stage + 1
        print(message)
        sys.exit(0)

    print("<<SWE_AGENT_SUBMISSION>>")
    print(patch)
    print("<<SWE_AGENT_SUBMISSION>>")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    # There are some super strange "ascii can't decode x" errors when printing to the terminal
    # that can be solved with setting the default encoding for stdout
    # (note that python3.6 doesn't have the reconfigure method)
    sys.stdout = io.TextIOWrapper(sys.stdout.buffer, encoding="utf-8")
    main()
